 Science of slow deep breathing
 There is robust scientific evidence for the benefits of mindful breathing
 Shallow breathing limits the diaphragms range of motion
 The lowest part of the lung doesn't get a full share of oxygenated air
 That can make you feel short of breath and anxious
 Deep abdominal breathing encourages full oxygen exchange, that is, the beneficial of incoming oxygen for outgoing carbon dioxide
 Not surprisingly it can slow the heartbeat and lower or stabilize blood pressure
 So the next time someone tells you to take a deep breath, smile, breathe deep and heed their wise advice as it instantly changes your state of mind and makes you feel happy

 rashtrapita mahatma gandhi jis alfred hai skool main padhe the, use band kar diya gaya he
 Leaving certificates have also been given to all 150 students studying in the school
 
 
 
 The foundation stone of Jamia was laid by this President, that this school is in Rajkot
 ab skool main notification jari kar ise band kar diya gaya he
 Why was the school closed? Actually, in 2016, the Gujarat government issued a notification informing that the school would be converted into a museum named after Mahatma Gandhi
 isamen kareeb 12 karod kaa kharch aayega
 That is why the children will be shifted to the Karanasinghi High School
 mahatma gandhi ko aupchaarik dhang se nahin mili he rashtrapita kii oopaadhi: sarkaarbta den ki ab chaatro ko leaving certificate de die gaye hai
 According to media reports, students and teachers will be removed from here by the end of this month
 kitna purana he schoolis skool kaa nirmaan british kaal main hua tha
 It was also the first English school in the region
 iskaa original naam rajkot english skool he
 It was established on October 17, 1853
 1868 se ise rajkot hai skool ke naam se janaa jane laga or phir 1907 main elfred hai skool ke naam se
